This logger allows loading shared object\\n22: // files via ``dlopen`` to implement custom access logging behavior.\\n23: //\\n24: // A module can be loaded by multiple access loggers; the module is loaded only once and shared\\n25: // across multiple logger instances.\\n26: //\\n27: // The access logger receives completed request information including request/response headers,\\n28: // stream info (timing, upstream info, response codes), and the log context type.\\n29: message DynamicModuleAccessLog {\\n30:   // Specifies the shared-object level configuration. If not specified, defaults to an empty string.\\n35:   //\\n36:   // This can be used to distinguish between different logger implementations inside a dynamic\\n37:   // module. For example, a module can have completely different logger implementations (e.g.,\\n38:   // file logger, gRPC logger, metrics logger). When Envoy receives this configuration, it passes\\n39:   // the ``logger_name`` to the dynamic module's access logger config init function together with\\n40:   // the ``logger_config``. That way a module can decide which in-module logger implementation to\\n41:   // use based on the name at load time.\\n42:   string logger_name = 2;\\n43: \\n44:   // The configuration for the logger chosen by ``logger_name``. `StatusCodeFilter`, `DurationFilter`, `AndFilter`, `OrFilter`, `NotHealthCheckFilter`, `TraceableRequestFilter`, `RuntimeFilter`, `HeaderFilter`, `ResponseFlagFilter`, `GrpcStatusFilter`, `LogTypeFilter`, `MetadataFilter`. Also contains `FilterFactory` and `AccessLogFactory`.\\n\\n**Access log manager** (source/common/access_log/access_log_manager_impl.h/.cc):\\nManages file-based access log file handles.\\n\\n#### source/extensions/access_loggers/common/\\n\\n- `access_log_base.h/.cc`: `ImplBase` — base class for all sink implementations, handles the filter evaluation before calling `emitLog()`.\\n- `file_access_log_impl.h/.cc`: `FileAccessLog` — sink that writes formatted log entries to a file (or stdout/stderr). Uses a `FormatterPtr` internally, so it supports both text and JSON depending on the formatter configured.\\n- `grpc_access_logger.h`: `GrpcAccessLogger` template — base for gRPC-based access log sinks.\\n- `grpc_access_logger_clients.h`: gRPC async client helpers for access loggers.\\n- `grpc_access_logger_utils.h/.cc`: Utilities for gRPC access log serialization.\\n- `stream_access_log_common_impl.h`: Template function `createStreamAccessLogInstance` shared by stdout/stderr loggers.\\n\\n#### source/extensions/access_loggers/file/ — File Access Logger\\n\\n- `config.h/.cc`: `FileAccessLogFactory` — factory registered as `envoy.access_loggers.file` (legacy: `envoy.file_access_log`). **Supports both structured (JSON) and unstructured (text) logging.** The `config.cc` switches on `access_log_format_case()` handling: `kFormat` (plain text, deprecated), `kJsonFormat` (JSON dict with string values, deprecated), `kTypedJsonFormat` (JSON dict with typed values, deprecated), and `kLogFormat` (modern `SubstitutionFormatString` supporting both text and JSON).\\n\\n#### source/extensions/access_loggers/grpc/ — gRPC Access Logger (ALS)\\n\\n- `http_config.h/.cc`: Factory for `envoy.access_loggers.http_grpc`.\\n- `tcp_config.h/.cc`: Factory for `envoy.access_loggers.tcp_grpc`.\\n- `http_grpc_access_log_impl.h/.cc`: `HttpGrpcAccessLog` — streams HTTP access log entries as structured Protobuf messages over gRPC to an ALS server. **Structured only** (no JSON; uses `HTTPAccessLogEntry` proto).\\n- `tcp_grpc_access_log_impl.h/.cc`: `TcpGrpcAccessLog` — streams TCP access log entries as structured Protobuf messages. **Structured only** (no JSON; uses `TCPAccessLogEntry` proto).\\n- `grpc_access_log_impl.h/.cc`: `GrpcAccessLoggerImpl`/`GrpcAccessLoggerCacheImpl` — shared logger/cache for gRPC-based access logging.\\n- `grpc_access_log_utils.h/.cc`, `grpc_access_log_proto_descriptors.h/.cc`, `config_utils.h/.cc`: Supporting utilities.\\n\\n#### source/extensions/access_loggers/fluentd/ — Fluentd Access Logger\\n\\n- `config.h/.cc`: Factory for `envoy.access_loggers.fluentd`.\\n- `fluentd_access_log_impl.h/.cc`: `FluentdAccessLog`, `FluentdAccessLoggerImpl`, `FluentdAccessLoggerCacheImpl` — sends log entries over TCP in Fluentd Forward Protocol (msgpack binary format). The record is configured as a `google.protobuf.Struct` with format substitution strings. **Structured only** (msgpack/JSON-like structured records, not plain text).\\n- `substitution_formatter.h/.cc`: `FluentdFormatter` — formats access log entries as msgpack records.\\n\\n#### source/extensions/access_loggers/open_telemetry/ — OpenTelemetry Access Logger\\n\\n- `config.h/.cc`: Factory for `envoy.access_loggers.open_telemetry`.\\n- `access_log_impl.h/.cc`: `AccessLog` — streams logs as OpenTelemetry `ExportLogsServiceRequest` over gRPC or HTTP. **Structured only** (OTel LogRecord format; body and attributes are key-value structured data).\\n- `grpc_access_log_impl.h/.cc`: OTel-specific gRPC logger.\\n- `substitution_formatter.h/.cc`: `OpenTelemetryFormatter` — formats access log entries as OTel `AnyValue`/`KeyValueList` structures.\\n- `access_log_proto_descriptors.h/.cc`: Proto descriptor registration.\\n\\n#### source/extensions/access_loggers/stream/ — stdout/stderr Access Loggers\\n\\n- `config.h/.cc`: `StdoutAccessLogFactory` (`envoy.access_loggers.stdout`) and `StderrAccessLogFactory` (`envoy.access_loggers.stderr`). **Supports both structured (JSON) and unstructured (text) logging** via `SubstitutionFormatString` (`log_format` field).\\n\\n#### source/extensions/access_loggers/wasm/ — WASM Access Logger\\n\\n- `config.h/.cc`: Factory for `envoy.access_loggers.wasm`.\\n- `wasm_access_log_impl.h`: `WasmAccessLog` — delegates log emission to a WebAssembly plugin. **Format determined by WASM plugin** (neither inherently text nor JSON).\\n\\n#### source/extensions/access_loggers/filters/cel/ — CEL Access Log Filter\\n\\n- `cel.h/.cc`: `CELAccessLogExtensionFilter` — access log **filter** (not a sink) that uses Common Expression Language to decide whether to emit a log entry. No output format.\\n- `config.h/.cc`: Factory for `envoy.access_loggers.extension_filters.cel`.\\n\\n---\\n\\n### Proto Definitions (envoyproxy/data-plane-api)\\n\\n1. **envoy/extensions/access_loggers/file/v3/file.proto** — `FileAccessLog`:\\n   Supports `format` (text, deprecated), `json_format` (JSON dict, deprecated), `typed_json_format` (typed JSON, deprecated), and `log_format` (SubstitutionFormatString — both text and JSON). **Supports structured JSON logging.**\\n\\n2. **envoy/extensions/access_loggers/grpc/v3/als.proto** — `HttpGrpcAccessLogConfig`, `TcpGrpcAccessLogConfig`, `CommonGrpcAccessLogConfig`:\\n   Sends structured Protobuf messages over gRPC ALS. **Structured (Protobuf), not text or JSON.**\\n\\n3. **envoy/extensions/access_loggers/fluentd/v3/fluentd.proto** — `FluentdAccessLogConfig`:\\n   Record field is a `google.protobuf.Struct` (structured JSON-like key-value map). Output is msgpack binary. **Structured logging (not plain text).**\\n\\n4. **envoy/extensions/access_loggers/open_telemetry/v3/logs_service.proto** — `OpenTelemetryAccessLogConfig`:\\n   Sends logs in OTel LogRecord format (body as `AnyValue`, attributes as `KeyValueList`). **Structured logging only.**\\n\\n5. **envoy/extensions/access_loggers/stream/v3/stream.proto** — `StdoutAccessLog`, `StderrAccessLog`:\\n   Uses `SubstitutionFormatString log_format`. **Supports both text and JSON structured logging.**\\n\\n6. **envoy/extensions/access_loggers/wasm/v3/wasm.proto** — `WasmAccessLog`:\\n   Delegates to a WASM `PluginConfig`. **Format is plugin-defined.**\\n\\n7. **envoy/extensions/access_loggers/filters/cel/v3/cel.proto** — `ExpressionFilter`:\\n   CEL-based access log filter (not a sink). No output format.\\n\\n8. **envoy/extensions/access_loggers/filters/process_ratelimit/v3/process_ratelimit.proto** — `ProcessRateLimitFilter`:\\n   Rate-limiting access log filter (not a sink). No output format.\\n\\n9. **envoy/extensions/access_loggers/stats/v3/stats.proto** — `Config`:\\n   Emits Envoy counters and histograms based on access log data. **Not a traditional log sink** — outputs Envoy stats metrics, not text or JSON log records.\\n\\n10. **envoy/extensions/access_loggers/dynamic_modules/v3/dynamic_modules.proto** — `DynamicModuleAccessLog`:\\n    Delegates to a native shared library loaded via `dlopen`. **Format is module-defined.** The `logger_config` field can pass JSON (`google.protobuf.Struct`) or string configuration to the module.\\n\\n---\\n\\n### Structured \"envoy/extensions/access_loggers/dynamic_modules/v3/dynamic_modules.proto\", \"symbol\": \"DynamicModuleAccessLog\"}\n  ],\n  \"text\": \"## Envoy Access Logging Infrastructure Audit\\n\\n### C++ Source Files\\n\\n#### source/common/access_log/\\n\\n**Access log filter implementations** (`source/common/access_log/access_log_impl.h/.cc`):\\nDefines the built-in access log filter types: `StatusCodeFilter`, `DurationFilter`, `AndFilter`, `OrFilter`, `NotHealthCheckFilter`, `TraceableRequestFilter`, `RuntimeFilter`, `HeaderFilter`, `ResponseFlagFilter`, `GrpcStatusFilter`, `LogTypeFilter`, `MetadataFilter`. Also provides `FilterFactory` and `AccessLogFactory`. These are filter-side, not output-side: they control which requests get logged, not how.\\n\\n**Access log manager** (`source/common/access_log/access_log_manager_impl.h/.cc`):\\nManages file handles for file-based access log sinks.\\n\\n#### source/extensions/access_loggers/common/\\n\\n- `access_log_base.h/.cc`: `ImplBase` - abstract base for all log sink implementations; calls `emitLog()` after filter check.\\n- `file_access_log_impl.h/.cc`: `FileAccessLog` - sink writing formatted entries to a file (or stdout/stderr). Accepts a `FormatterPtr`, so it supports both text and JSON depending on configuration.\\n- `grpc_access_logger.h`: `GrpcAccessLogger` template - base for gRPC-based sink implementations.\\n- `grpc_access_logger_clients.h`: gRPC async client helpers.\\n- `grpc_access_logger_utils.h/.cc`: Utilities for gRPC access log serialization.\\n- `stream_access_log_common_impl.h`: Template helper `createStreamAccessLogInstance` shared by stdout/stderr loggers.\\n\\n#### source/extensions/access_loggers/file/ - File Access Logger\\n\\n- `config.h/.cc`: `FileAccessLogFactory` registered as `envoy.access_loggers.file` (legacy: `envoy.file_access_log`). **Supports both structured (JSON) and unstructured (text) logging.** The factory switches on `access_log_format_case()` handling: `kFormat` (plain text, deprecated), `kJsonFormat` (JSON dict string values, deprecated), `kTypedJsonFormat` (typed JSON, deprecated), and `kLogFormat` (modern `SubstitutionFormatString` supporting text, JSON, and other formats).\\n\\n#### source/extensions/access_loggers/grpc/ - gRPC Access Logger (ALS)\\n\\n- `http_config.h/.cc`: Factory for `envoy.access_loggers.http_grpc`.\\n- `tcp_config.h/.cc`: Factory for `envoy.access_loggers.tcp_grpc`.\\n- `http_grpc_access_log_impl.h/.cc`: `HttpGrpcAccessLog` - streams HTTP access log entries as structured Protobuf messages (`HTTPAccessLogEntry`) over gRPC to an ALS server. **Structured Protobuf only; no JSON or plain text output.**\\n- `tcp_grpc_access_log_impl.h/.cc`: `TcpGrpcAccessLog` - streams TCP access log entries as structured Protobuf messages (`TCPAccessLogEntry`). **Structured Protobuf only.**\\n- `grpc_access_log_impl.h/.cc`: `GrpcAccessLoggerImpl`/`GrpcAccessLoggerCacheImpl` - shared logger/cache.\\n- `grpc_access_log_utils.h/.cc`, `grpc_access_log_proto_descriptors.h/.cc`, `config_utils.h/.cc`: Supporting utilities.\\n\\n#### source/extensions/access_loggers/fluentd/ - Fluentd Access Logger\\n\\n- `config.h/.cc`: Factory for `envoy.access_loggers.fluentd`.\\n- `fluentd_access_log_impl.h/.cc`: `FluentdAccessLog`, `FluentdAccessLoggerImpl`, `FluentdAccessLoggerCacheImpl` - sends log entries over TCP in Fluentd Forward Protocol (msgpack binary format). The record is configured as a `google.protobuf.Struct` with substitution format strings as values. **Structured only** (msgpack binary with JSON-like structured key-value records; not plain text).\\n- `substitution_formatter.h/.cc`: `FluentdFormatter` - produces msgpack-encoded records from access log context.\\n\\n#### source/extensions/access_loggers/open_telemetry/ - OpenTelemetry Access Logger\\n\\n- `config.h/.cc`: Factory for `envoy.access_loggers.open_telemetry`.\\n- `access_log_impl.h/.cc`: `AccessLog` - streams logs as OpenTelemetry `ExportLogsServiceRequest` over gRPC or HTTP. **Structured only** (OTel LogRecord format; body as `AnyValue`, attributes as `KeyValueList`).\\n- `grpc_access_log_impl.h/.cc`: OTel-specific gRPC logger.\\n- `substitution_formatter.h/.cc`: `OpenTelemetryFormatter` - formats access log entries into OTel structured data.\\n- `access_log_proto_descriptors.h/.cc`: Proto descriptor registration.\\n\\n#### source/extensions/access_loggers/stream/ - stdout/stderr Access Loggers\\n\\n- `config.h/.cc`: `StdoutAccessLogFactory` (`envoy.access_loggers.stdout`, legacy: `envoy.stdout_access_log`) and `StderrAccessLogFactory` (`envoy.access_loggers.stderr`, legacy: `envoy.stderr_access_log`). **Supports both structured (JSON) and unstructured (text) logging** via the `log_format` field (`SubstitutionFormatString`).\\n\\n#### source/extensions/access_loggers/wasm/ - WASM Access Logger\\n\\n- `config.h/.cc`: Factory for `envoy.access_loggers.wasm`.\\n- `wasm_access_log_impl.h`: `WasmAccessLog` - delegates log emission to a WebAssembly plugin via `wasm()->log()`. **Format entirely determined by the WASM plugin.**\\n\\n#### source/extensions/access_loggers/filters/cel/ - CEL Access Log Filter\\n\\n- `cel.h/.cc`: `CELAccessLogExtensionFilter` - access log **filter** (not a sink) using Common Expression Language to decide whether to emit a log. No output format of its own.\\n- `config.h/.cc`: Factory for `envoy.access_loggers.extension_filters.cel`.\\n\\n---\\n\\n### Proto Definitions (envoyproxy/data-plane-api)\\n\\n1. **`envoy/extensions/access_loggers/file/v3/file.proto`** - `FileAccessLog`: Supports `format` (text, deprecated), `json_format` (JSON dict, deprecated), `typed_json_format` (typed JSON, deprecated), and `log_format` (`SubstitutionFormatString` - text and JSON). **Supports both structured JSON and unstructured text.**\\n\\n2. **`envoy/extensions/access_loggers/grpc/v3/als.proto`** - `HttpGrpcAccessLogConfig`, `TcpGrpcAccessLogConfig`, `CommonGrpcAccessLogConfig`: Sends structured Protobuf messages over gRPC ALS. **Structured Protobuf; not text or JSON.**\\n\\n3. **`envoy/extensions/access_loggers/fluentd/v3/fluentd.proto`** - `FluentdAccessLogConfig`: Record field is `google.protobuf.Struct` (structured JSON-like key-value map with substitution format string values). Output is msgpack binary. **Structured logging only; not plain text.**\\n\\n4. **`envoy/extensions/access_loggers/open_telemetry/v3/logs_service.proto`** - `OpenTelemetryAccessLogConfig`: Sends logs in OTel LogRecord format (`body` as `AnyValue`, `attributes` as `KeyValueList`). **Structured logging only.**\\n\\n5. **`envoy/extensions/access_loggers/stream/v3/stream.proto`** - `StdoutAccessLog`, `StderrAccessLog`: Uses `SubstitutionFormatString log_format`. **Supports both structured (JSON) and unstructured (text) logging.**\\n\\n6. **`envoy/extensions/access_loggers/wasm/v3/wasm.proto`** - `WasmAccessLog`: Delegates to a WASM `PluginConfig`. **Format is plugin-defined.**\\n\\n7. **`envoy/extensions/access_loggers/filters/cel/v3/cel.proto`** - `ExpressionFilter`: CEL-based access log filter (not a sink). No output format.\\n\\n8. **`envoy/extensions/access_loggers/filters/process_ratelimit/v3/process_ratelimit.proto`** - `ProcessRateLimitFilter`: Rate-limiting access log filter using a dynamic token bucket (not a sink). No output format.\\n\\n9. **`envoy/extensions/access_loggers/stats/v3/stats.proto`** - `Config`: Emits Envoy counters and histograms derived from access log data. **Not a traditional text/JSON log sink** - outputs Envoy metrics, not log records.\\n\\n10. **`envoy/extensions/access_loggers/dynamic_modules/v3/dynamic_modules.proto`** - `DynamicModuleAccessLog`: Delegates to a native shared library loaded via `dlopen`. **Format is module-defined.** Configuration can be passed as JSON (`google.protobuf.Struct`), bytes, or string.\\n\\n---\\n\\n### Structured vs. Unstructured Logging Summary\\n\\n| Extension name | Type | Structured JSON | Unstructured Text | Notes |\\n|---|---|---|---|---|\\n| envoy.access_loggers.file | Sink | YES | YES | json_format, typed_json_format, log_format (SubstitutionFormatString) |\\n| envoy.access_loggers.stdout | Sink | YES | YES | log_format (SubstitutionFormatString) |\\n| envoy.access_loggers.stderr | Sink | YES | YES | log_format (SubstitutionFormatString) |\\n| envoy.access_loggers.http_grpc | Sink | NO | NO | Structured Protobuf (HTTPAccessLogEntry) over gRPC ALS |\\n| envoy.access_loggers.tcp_grpc | Sink | NO | NO | Source Files\\n\\n#### source/common/access_log/\\n\\n**Access log filter implementations** (`source/common/access_log/access_log_impl.h/.cc`):\\nDefines the built-in access log filter types: `StatusCodeFilter`, `DurationFilter`, `AndFilter`, `OrFilter`, `NotHealthCheckFilter`, `TraceableRequestFilter`, `RuntimeFilter`, `HeaderFilter`, `ResponseFlagFilter`, `GrpcStatusFilter`, `LogTypeFilter`, `MetadataFilter`. Also provides `FilterFactory` and `AccessLogFactory`. These are filter-side, not output-side: they control which requests get logged, not how.\\n\\n**Access log manager** (`source/common/access_log/access_log_manager_impl.h/.cc`):\\nManages file handles for file-based access log sinks.\\n\\n#### source/extensions/access_loggers/common/\\n\\n- `access_log_base.h/.cc`: `ImplBase` - abstract base for all log sink implementations; calls `emitLog()` after filter check.\\n- `file_access_log_impl.h/.cc`: `FileAccessLog` - sink writing formatted entries to a file (or stdout/stderr). Accepts a `FormatterPtr`, so it supports both text and JSON depending on configuration.\\n- `grpc_access_logger.h`: `GrpcAccessLogger` template - base for gRPC-based sink implementations.\\n- `grpc_access_logger_clients.h`: gRPC async client helpers.\\n- `grpc_access_logger_utils.h/.cc`: Utilities for gRPC access log serialization.\\n- `stream_access_log_common_impl.h`: Template helper `createStreamAccessLogInstance` shared by stdout/stderr loggers.\\n\\n#### source/extensions/access_loggers/file/ - File Access Logger\\n\\n- `config.h/.cc`: `FileAccessLogFactory` registered as `envoy.access_loggers.file` (legacy: `envoy.file_access_log`). **Supports both structured (JSON) and unstructured (text) logging.** The factory switches on `access_log_format_case()` handling: `kFormat` (plain text, deprecated), `kJsonFormat` (JSON dict string values, deprecated), `kTypedJsonFormat` (typed JSON, deprecated), and `kLogFormat` (modern `SubstitutionFormatString` supporting text, JSON, and other formats).\\n\\n#### source/extensions/access_loggers/grpc/ - gRPC Access Logger (ALS)\\n\\n- `http_config.h/.cc`: Factory for `envoy.access_loggers.http_grpc`.\\n- `tcp_config.h/.cc`: Factory for `envoy.access_loggers.tcp_grpc`.\\n- `http_grpc_access_log_impl.h/.cc`: `HttpGrpcAccessLog` - streams HTTP access log entries as structured Protobuf messages (`HTTPAccessLogEntry`) over gRPC to an ALS server. **Structured Protobuf only; no JSON or plain text output.**\\n- `tcp_grpc_access_log_impl.h/.cc`: `TcpGrpcAccessLog` - streams TCP access log entries as structured Protobuf messages (`TCPAccessLogEntry`). **Structured Protobuf only.**\\n- `grpc_access_log_impl.h/.cc`: `GrpcAccessLoggerImpl`/`GrpcAccessLoggerCacheImpl` - shared logger/cache.\\n- `grpc_access_log_utils.h/.cc`, `grpc_access_log_proto_descriptors.h/.cc`, `config_utils.h/.cc`: Supporting utilities.\\n\\n#### source/extensions/access_loggers/fluentd/ - Fluentd Access Logger\\n\\n- `config.h/.cc`: Factory for `envoy.access_loggers.fluentd`.\\n- `fluentd_access_log_impl.h/.cc`: `FluentdAccessLog`, `FluentdAccessLoggerImpl`, `FluentdAccessLoggerCacheImpl` - sends log entries over TCP in Fluentd Forward Protocol (msgpack binary format). The record is configured as a `google.protobuf.Struct` with substitution format strings as values. **Structured only** (msgpack binary with JSON-like structured key-value records; not plain text).\\n- `substitution_formatter.h/.cc`: `FluentdFormatter` - produces msgpack-encoded records from access log context.\\n\\n#### source/extensions/access_loggers/open_telemetry/ - OpenTelemetry Access Logger\\n\\n- `config.h/.cc`: Factory for `envoy.access_loggers.open_telemetry`.\\n- `access_log_impl.h/.cc`: `AccessLog` - streams logs as OpenTelemetry `ExportLogsServiceRequest` over gRPC or HTTP. **Structured only** (OTel LogRecord format; body as `AnyValue`, attributes as `KeyValueList`).\\n- `grpc_access_log_impl.h/.cc`: OTel-specific gRPC logger.\\n- `substitution_formatter.h/.cc`: `OpenTelemetryFormatter` - formats access log entries into OTel structured data.\\n- `access_log_proto_descriptors.h/.cc`: Proto descriptor registration.\\n\\n#### source/extensions/access_loggers/stream/ - stdout/stderr Access Loggers\\n\\n- `config.h/.cc`: `StdoutAccessLogFactory` (`envoy.access_loggers.stdout`, legacy: `envoy.stdout_access_log`) and `StderrAccessLogFactory` (`envoy.access_loggers.stderr`, legacy: `envoy.stderr_access_log`). **Supports both structured (JSON) and unstructured (text) logging** via the `log_format` field (`SubstitutionFormatString`).\\n\\n#### source/extensions/access_loggers/wasm/ - WASM Access Logger\\n\\n- `config.h/.cc`: Factory for `envoy.access_loggers.wasm`.\\n- `wasm_access_log_impl.h`: `WasmAccessLog` - delegates log emission to a WebAssembly plugin via `wasm()->log()`. **Format entirely determined by the WASM plugin.**\\n\\n#### source/extensions/access_loggers/filters/cel/ - CEL Access Log Filter\\n\\n- `cel.h/.cc`: `CELAccessLogExtensionFilter` - access log **filter** (not a sink) using Common Expression Language to decide whether to emit a log. No output format of its own.\\n- `config.h/.cc`: Factory for `envoy.access_loggers.extension_filters.cel`.\\n\\n---\\n\\n### Proto Definitions (envoyproxy/data-plane-api)\\n\\n1. **`envoy/extensions/access_loggers/file/v3/file.proto`** - `FileAccessLog`: Supports `format` (text, deprecated), `json_format` (JSON dict, deprecated), `typed_json_format` (typed JSON, deprecated), and `log_format` (`SubstitutionFormatString` - text and JSON). **Supports both structured JSON and unstructured text.**\\n\\n2. **`envoy/extensions/access_loggers/grpc/v3/als.proto`** - `HttpGrpcAccessLogConfig`, `TcpGrpcAccessLogConfig`, `CommonGrpcAccessLogConfig`: Sends structured Protobuf messages over gRPC ALS. **Structured Protobuf; not text or JSON.**\\n\\n3. **`envoy/extensions/access_loggers/fluentd/v3/fluentd.proto`** - `FluentdAccessLogConfig`: Record field is `google.protobuf.Struct` (structured JSON-like key-value map with substitution format string values). Output is msgpack binary. **Structured logging only; not plain text.**\\n\\n4. **`envoy/extensions/access_loggers/open_telemetry/v3/logs_service.proto`** - `OpenTelemetryAccessLogConfig`: Sends logs in OTel LogRecord format (`body` as `AnyValue`, `attributes` as `KeyValueList`). **Structured logging only.**\\n\\n5. **`envoy/extensions/access_loggers/stream/v3/stream.proto`** - `StdoutAccessLog`, `StderrAccessLog`: Uses `SubstitutionFormatString log_format`. **Supports both structured (JSON) and unstructured (text) logging.**\\n\\n6. **`envoy/extensions/access_loggers/wasm/v3/wasm.proto`** - `WasmAccessLog`: Delegates to a WASM `PluginConfig`. **Format is plugin-defined.**\\n\\n7. **`envoy/extensions/access_loggers/filters/cel/v3/cel.proto`** - `ExpressionFilter`: CEL-based access log filter (not a sink). No output format.\\n\\n8. **`envoy/extensions/access_loggers/filters/process_ratelimit/v3/process_ratelimit.proto`** - `ProcessRateLimitFilter`: Rate-limiting access log filter using a dynamic token bucket (not a sink). No output format.\\n\\n9. **`envoy/extensions/access_loggers/stats/v3/stats.proto`** - `Config`: Emits Envoy counters and histograms derived from access log data. **Not a traditional text/JSON log sink** - outputs Envoy metrics, not log records.\\n\\n10. **`envoy/extensions/access_loggers/dynamic_modules/v3/dynamic_modules.proto`** - `DynamicModuleAccessLog`: Delegates to a native shared library loaded via `dlopen`. **Format is module-defined.** Configuration can be passed as JSON (`google.protobuf.Struct`), bytes, or string.\\n\\n---\\n\\n### Structured vs. Unstructured Logging Summary\\n\\n| Extension name | Type | Structured JSON | Unstructured Text | Notes |\\n|---|---|---|---|---|\\n| envoy.access_loggers.file | Sink | YES | YES | json_format, typed_json_format, log_format (SubstitutionFormatString) |\\n| envoy.access_loggers.stdout | Sink | YES | YES | log_format (SubstitutionFormatString) |\\n| envoy.access_loggers.stderr | Sink | YES | YES | log_format (SubstitutionFormatString) |\\n| envoy.access_loggers.http_grpc | Sink | NO | NO | Structured Protobuf (HTTPAccessLogEntry) over gRPC ALS |\\n| envoy.access_loggers.tcp_grpc | Sink | NO | NO | Structured Protobuf (TCPAccessLogEntry) over gRPC ALS |\\n| envoy.access_loggers.fluentd | Sink | YES (msgpack) | NO | Structured msgpack records from Struct config |\\n| envoy.access_loggers.open_telemetry | Sink | YES (OTel) | NO | OTel LogRecord format over gRPC or HTTP |\\n| envoy.access_loggers.wasm | Sink | plugin-defined | plugin-defined | Delegates to WASM plugin |\\n| envoy.access_loggers.stats | Sink | NO | NO | Emits Envoy counters/histograms, not log records |\\n| envoy.access_loggers.dynamic_modules | Sink | module-defined | module-defined | Delegates to native shared library |\\n| envoy.access_loggers.extension_filters.cel | Filter | N/A | N/A | Filter only, controls which requests are logged |\\n| envoy.access_loggers.extension_filters.process_ratelimit | Filter | N/A | N/A | Filter only, rate-limits log emission |\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
